< rating>
3<//rating>
<Text>I was craving for some taco truck food and found this place thru Yelp. It was easy enough to find and the customer service was pretty quick and the guys working were friendly.

I was very hungry and decided to try a bunch of their menu items. I ordered a Mexican style hot dog, steak fries, and four tacos each with a different meat. The hot dog was meh. It had some kick from the peppers on top but I really didn't taste much of the sausage or the bacon that it was wrapped in. The steak fries were just ok too. The fries weren't really crispy and the steak felt dry. The green chili sauce added a lot of flavor and really made up for everything else. It was definitely filling. All four tacos were pretty standard, I didnt feel like they wowed me. The steak one was, again, dry. The birria had nice flavor but it felt muted compared to other birria I've had. The pastor wasn't very flavorful to me. The cabeza was easily my favorite part of the meal. It was flavorful, tender and made for a satisfying two-bite taco.

Overall, I would say I didn't go completely crazy about this place and its food. It wasn't really bad by any means but it definitely didn't fulfill my taco truck cravings. Maybe I came on an off night, I would probably try it again later should it cross my mind.</Text><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO5P9XV7fwCXCHB0T7eO6L4Mn2AbVL_wGkh-wBg=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOV6LbfJMbf3cV-uUNM_KuORARk4iPrKZTvX_LH=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPJCQ6u6LHiwrGEP_pfWTbP2NJ5XX-Npn8xl0jl=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pictures><Response>None</Response>< gmap_id>

< text>
I honestly wish I could rate this office by category. The doctor and clinical assistant are awesome. Knowledgeable, Caring, Friendly. Great back office experience. 5 stars.  Dealing with the front office staff, that's why I ended up leaving the practice.  As someone who works in healthcare I know that the office experience starts at the initial phone call, when I called to make my appointment I was not impressed with the phone etiquette, I should've known from there it was all down hill.  My initial visit with the office didn't fare any better, I cut them a lot of slack due to Covid but the front office staff didn't seem to know what they were doing, after coming out of the exam with the doctor I needed to pick out glasses and dealt with the office manager of whom I was not looking forward to seeing as I had earlier witnessed her yelling at staff in front of patient's waiting in the lobby. It was unprofessional and verbally abusive. When I came back to pick up my glasses they couldn't find them and said they couldn't find me, was I a patient there. I assured her that I knew this and was going to pay out of pocket and she looked at me as if I was lying. I pre-paid for my contacts and left only to return once again when they called me that they had arrive and once again they couldn't find them and was I called to pick them up? Even after all of this I kept trying to go back. I've stopped by the office to reorder contacts but was told they were at lunch, even though it wasn't 12pm yet and wouldn't let me order, I left several messages, and no one has called me back.  Finally today I scheduled an appointment with another office in town and if the initial call is any indication, I am going to be very happy with that office.</text>

<user_name>Rudy Namikis</user_name><time>1569218694644<//time>< rate>

<Review>Tina's is literally overflowing with character. Not only is the building thoroughly decorated, but Tina herself is an amazingly charismatic woman with tremendous stories of her life. Make sure to ask about how she survived as the 11th kid in a poor family in the Philippines!

The food is homemade and very delicious, with filling portions.

Depending on the season, Tina might just offer you a fresh, hand-picked guava. Take it!

Tina's is the full-spectrum antidote to the excess of chain restaurants and sanitized consumerism that plague our country. In many ways, I felt like I was back in 1910, grabbing a bite after a hard day in the oil fields and chatting with the owner.< /Review><Pics>None<//Pics>< resp>

< Text>
I won't be returning to the Paul Mitchell School - Costa Mesa. I didn't go in with high expectations because I knew these were students, but I was very disappointed about how inconsiderate they were of my time and feelings. I went in for a trim and highlights, they said they would definitely be able to complete it all in a timely manner. I came in at 6:30pm and left at 10:30pm, 4 hours! I was so exhausted, frustrated, and angry by the time I left. They rushed my haircut too because by 9:45am they hadn't even started the cut. I could have been told that from the beginning! I would have said just a cut please.

Within the first hour all the student had done was part my hair and test 1 strip of hair for color. I know she's learning, but I was hoping the instructor would come to assist her and let her know to be more conscious of time. The whole time she was aware of my frustration and how slow she was going, but she didn't make the effort to ask for help to speed up the process. Instructor knew the situation and didn't assist, many times I saw her sitting in a chair chatting with others. My cut done by the instructor near the end and was rushed, nothing impressive... I just got a trim and bangs. The teasing of the hair was a bit rough... The instructor tried to teach her how to be gentle, but she couldn't grasp it.

No discount either. All the instructor said was "I won't charge you for the extra bowl of dye" and "thank you for your patience". You mean the extra bowl the student didn't need to use, but she used because she doesn't know how to conserve her supplies properly? That isn't my fault at all and not much of a "discount", this should be incorporate into the general cost of the school because obviously learning students will use more supplies, not as the customer's expense. The haircut took 4 hours and was nothing too difficult, but still cost over $60. Would rather pay more to spend less time in the salon and get a better cut & service.

The student was very pleasant and sweet, which is why I won't name her, but I hope she learns to speed up, be aware of the customer's time, and approach others for help.</Text>

I was so exhausted, frustrated, and angry by the time I left. They rushed my haircut too because by 9:45am they hadn't even started the cut. I could have been told that from the beginning! I would have said just a cut please.

Within the first hour all the student had done was part my hair and test 1 strip of hair for color. I know she's learning, but I was hoping the instructor would come to assist her and let her know to be more conscious of time. The whole time she was aware of my frustration and how slow she was going, but she didn't make the effort to ask for help to speed up the process. Instructor knew the situation and didn't assist, many times I saw her sitting in a chair chatting with others. My cut done by the instructor near the end and was rushed, nothing impressive... I just got a trim and bangs. The teasing of the hair was a bit rough... The instructor tried to teach her how to be gentle, but she couldn't grasp it.

No discount either. All the instructor said was "I won't charge you for the extra bowl of dye" and "thank you for your patience". You mean the extra bowl the student didn't need to use, but she used because she doesn't know how to conserve her supplies properly? That isn't my fault at all and not much of a "discount", this should be incorporate into the general cost of the school because obviously learning students will use more supplies, not as the customer's expense. The haircut took 4 hours and was nothing too difficult, but still cost over $60. Would rather pay more to spend less time in the salon and get a better cut & service.

The student was very pleasant and sweet, which is why I won't name her, but I hope she learns to speed up, be aware of the customer's time, and approach others for help.< /review>

< Review>
Fun place hard to find hidden between homes next to lake. Live music today was very good 60's - 70's. Food was delicious and portions where large. Full bar and outdoor large patio next to lake.limited parking lot some street parking. Lots of people here having fun. Motorcycle clubs meet here for food, drink and dancing.  Lots of room for party's or groups. Boat dock attached to back of bar for boating stop and pick up of food and drinks. In the area fun place. Ice tea was very good. Huge selection of beverages from the large bar. Table service was a little slow but understandably very busy fun place on the weekend.< /Review>

< Review>
It seems the restaurant is under new management as of Feb. 2020 (just in time for the Shelter in Place) and my experiences there all occurred previously to the change.  I'll have to drag myself in there when the Corona thing has passed (if they are still open) and write an updated review.  So take this for what it's worth.

The boathouse is a great place if you like to drink at the bar or come up from the water in a boat to drink on the deck.  They certainly seem to try hard at making a nice restaurant looking at the menu items and selection but when the place is absolutely empty except for your party and it takes over an hour to serve three main dishes and they are cold and stale you have to wonder what the problem is.  At least this has been my experience about a dozen times over the last 4-5 years.

Sure the dining room is quite dated and could use a deep cleaning, I don't mind that.  Also, the staff seem like well meaning people who are trying their best but if you're gonna run a restaurant the guests need hot fresh food in a timely manner.  Now if you're a drinker perhaps you can knock back a couple of high balls and by the time the food comes you're too buzzed to care that it's not hot or it has been an hour and a half after you received your salad/soup/app or isn't fresh and flavorful even if there are only the three or four of your group in the entire restaurant.  In fact reading through some of the 5 star reviews you might notice how many times the 'great bartender' is mentioned or the pool table or that many of the food items mentioned are basically deep fried bar food..

Now the place does have a pretty regular and busy section but that is in the bar/deck.  Since I haven't been a drinker in a long time I couldn't comment on that part but they do seem to be having a pretty good time by the sound.  The Boat House to me is like an old school Bar and Grill where the grill is there when the bar crowd need something to eat long after the Happy Hour has past.    My best experiences have been ordering take out and would suggest this to anyone focused on the food.  Sure it's usually cold by the time you get it home but you expect that.  They also generally have it ready to go when you show up.

I'm not trying to be negative this is just my honest in my assessment.  I've worked in nearly a dozen restaurants over the years and eaten at a few too.  I also live about three blocks from the place.  The only reason I've frequented the place regularly is that my parents always want to go there when visiting because it's on the lake, despite my protestations.</Review>

<GmapID>0x8083e84859f93f01:0x240c8f59b149de94< /GmapID><response>None</response><rate>3< /rate><user_name>Ralphghanistan</user_name></record></dataset><record>
<user_id>114713462113277205212</user_id>< Name>
Featherbed Railroad Bed & Breakfast< /Name>
< date>
1385652739709<//date>
< rate>
5< /rate>
< review>
The Boathouse has been a staple for guests for some time now but recently new management took over the kitchen and really stepped up the menu and service. The food can best be described as comfort food with barbecue as well and a number of intriguing daily specials. There's a full bar as well with a view of Clear Lake plus outdoor seating in the summer with bands featured  on Sunday afternoons.

Recently we had some sandwiches delivered which is usually unremarkable but I happened to get the tri tip sandwich. Bottom line, the tri tip had a wonderful smoky flavor and was as tender as can be. I avoid tri tip sandwiches because you usually end up with gristle surprise which ruins the experience - not in this case. It was tender and meaty from bite one to the end. The only disappointment was having finished the sandwich, darnit. But they'll make more!

We have sent many guests down the street to the Boathouse and have heard plenty of very positive reviews of the food and service. Being regulars ourselves we can attest to the warm atmosphere of this local hangout. The food is consistent and good, prices are very fair and service is generally quite good as well. We're pretty fortunate to have such a cool local hangout just a few steps down the street from us.<//review>
